2025-11-15T12:26:42.8348700Z ##[debug]    macro incorrectly, causing a compilation error. It also failed to
2025-11-15T12:26:42.8349217Z ##[debug]    include a space between the OSC path and the type tag string, which
2025-11-15T12:26:42.8349724Z ##[debug]    prevented the `from_str` method from parsing the output correctly.
2025-11-15T12:26:42.8350095Z ##[debug]
2025-11-15T12:26:42.8350448Z ##[debug]    This commit fixes the `to_string` implementation by using `format!` to
2025-11-15T12:26:42.8350940Z ##[debug]    build the string representation of the arguments. It also updates the
2025-11-15T12:26:42.8351461Z ##[debug]    tests and doctests to reflect the corrected string format.
